besturring himselfe great liuelinesse courage quéene sawe readinesse battaile gracious laughter sayd would neuer haue thought bene great ouersight knight especiallye fame without feare great number cannot abide procure euill possible without care high way doth put himselfe sléep tinacrian answered said great ouersight care venture selfe whereas shall receiue little profite doth séeme vnto thée ouerséene therein possibly thou wilt iudge contrary thou wilte proue strength arme cannot much conformable vnto thy ouersight saide faire ladie beléeue woulde gréeue make anye proofe thée great vertue thy fame dooth beare report therefore take thée thy horse let either v procure make defence héere doo aduise thée none knight hethertoo thou hast proued grecia mean time saying word tinacrian much behold although verie angrie wordes spoken▪ yet sayde well séeing thy follye doth much constraine thée make controuersie without occasion tarrie thou shalt sée howe wont punish foolish people thou arte great hast hée called horse straight waye brought vnto macedonio without putting foote stirroppe leaped saddle tooke speare hand without replying thing valiant tinacrian presently withdrew himselfe backe tooke field part néedfull lyke quéene one time returned light horse great hast stroke horse spur without pitie extreame furie made incounter vpon shéelds speares shiuered péeces passed along course without stay body mouing saddle turned aboute horse great lightnes sword hand quéene stroke first blowe prince shée made sparkes flye helme prince decline head saddle bow great lightnes settle himselfe againe saddle cleare himselfe second blow readie discharged vpon putting himselfe one side stroke blow vpon helme made great sound throughout field craggie mountaines shée fell backwards vpon horse crouper heade quickly arose vp againe settled selfe great yre layd fast holde vpon sword strike enimie finde idle rather began assault blowes mortall battaile blowes stroke betwixt least thought either make ende controuersie time came way knight armed rich armour strong mightie brufaldoro doo remember ye mightie strong blow giuen tinacrian remained alongst floore galley without remembrance came vnto himselfe accustomed brauery would followe way barke went calling remembrance great trauaile sorrow lady loue constraine follow owne iourney came thether vnderstood poliphebo set lybertie caried towards almaine court way trauailed met people tell happened signes token knight carried away lady vnderstand enemye left owne armour armed himselfe bramarants followed way tolde went fame tinacrian left behinde wheresoeuer came wheresoeuer went alwayes newes way trauailed vntill time came found battel worthy quéene staid behold battaile well fought length knew well knight brought great extremitie looking beholding battaile amongest rest knewe louing wife although ioye great séeing yet wrath ire knight much without saying word vnto quéene wife went toward battaile sword drawen hand put himselfe quéene sayde doo desire thée gentle knight thou wouldest rest take thine ease let alone strong arme take reuengement knight vsurper louing wife robber fame honour without detainment went strike mortall blowes worthy gentlewoman great anger said stand away knight let make ende haue begun offer wrong vnto doo knowe make demaund vnto thy cost therewith put selfe furious pagan great desire make reuengement turned put himselfe queene striking tinacrian mightie strong blowes much maruell neither one assaulted pagan meruailous mightie blow queene time put selfe againe vpon executed blow vpon left shoulder grieue much appeared outward countenaunce time pagan put himselfe againe formost furious lady sword aloft said keepe thy selfe backe thou vile knight base linage let make ende haue begun potencye arme doo ouerthrow thy great pride stand thou back sayde pagan right take vengeaunce euill knight doth carry lady robbed word spoken tinacrian know ye king mauritania brought great extremitie beginning knighthood full yre wrath insomuch thicke smoke came forth beauer time came vnto place claridiano speare light knighthood armed purple armour haue told departed emperor pallaice great secret saw great cō tention betwixt knight desirous know occasion put himselfe betwéene desired leaue battell furious pagan answered thou knight put thy self vnderstand matter thou art called thou dost possibly thou shalt beare part vnfortunate knight dooth owe claridiano said know wherein indebted vnto thée rather doo vnderstand thou art hath least reason knight branch first begun battaile first griefe sayd pagan gaue vnto order knighthood giuen defie mortall battaile content héerwith hath robbed ladye thou dost sée yonder word tinacrian answered said thou liest like euill knight yt haue robbed haue deliuered place whence thou thy power wert sufficient deliuer thy falshood thou shalt carrie away without mortall battell furious pagan heard ill spoken like lion went stoute dame put selfe said stand back pagan importunate diuell first thou shalt haue doo el thou shalt let make ende pretence braue tinacrian like furious lion said vnto ye gréeke prince curteous knight pray stand backe somewhat let alone doe estéeme thē little loude voice said come come thou pagan king little valour take companie thée arrogant foole thou art together meane set agréement ye strength force indomable arme claridiano sayd shall first procure cléere thy selfe branch set thée libertie pagan therewith drew sword stroke blow yt made tremble remain one amazed séeing ye case stroke another blow vpon beuer made pagan grype fast horse neck kéepe himselfe falling moore came quickly himselfe furious courage stroke vpon left sholder blow made gréeke shrinke body stoope downe saddle bow ye great griefe felle giuing terrible grone lift vp sword stroke pagan blow vpon ye helme spark fire flewe aire almost without remembrance fell vppon horse crupper pagan comming vnto selfe puffed beuer thick smoke threw shéeld back stroke gréeke terrible blowe without remembrance fell forward vpon horse eares carried vp ye field presently came againe vnto himselfe séeing yt ill intreated tooke sword hand set spur horse side made run lyke vnto winde straight pagan stroke blow semed whole tower falne vpon hauing power contrary fell vpon horse neck without anye feeling scarred terrible blow swift course carried master enimy time tinacrian faire dame idle saw battaile begun betwixt two knight great furie returned vnto battaile tinacrian full anger threwe shéeld backe stroke quéene mightie blow great fury yt made fall downe vpon buttock horse without remembrance caried round field quéene came quickly againe vnto selfe wrathfull thought take reuengement enimie throwing shield grounde tooke sworde hand stroke horse spurres made run like vnto winde trice shée tinacrian stroke vppon healme fire slew thereat lost sight valiant young knight fell backwardes vppon horse crupper without féelyng carried vp field lady saw would haue finished battaile another rigorous blow time fell horse valiaunt african master likewise runne field occasion gréeke might behold passed trice sayd withdraw thy selfe part heroycall knight pursue follow without remembrance lady angry gaue gréeke aunswere furious blow straight way paid ye like wher betwixt began new battaile meane time tinacrian pagan come againe vnto themselues setled saddle either looked aduersary beheld mortall battaile two together hate deadly made reckoning late enimies assalted one another furiously strongly great profit vnto quéene lira tinacrian mightie furious haue bene great perill cannot tell furious two warrior say claridiano verye sore wounded ouercome héereafter shall tolde sort medicine might auaile helpe thus indured foure houres without taking rest fighting fiercely beginning controuersie towardes part next sea side saw comming rosicleer stout troyan prince meridian séeing battaile stay behold rosicleer knew straight wayes armour bramarant seeing power another full wrath without tarrying put himselfe midst among furious voyce sayd tell knight made thée bold take armour place wheras put tropheo remembraunce pagan aunswered said superbious proud knight art thou fortune one gréeke prince great threatenings dost defende armour one said rosicleer take away thy life thy boldnesse therewith drew sword assault tinacrian put himselfe said great curtesie vnto elder brother knight prince grecia let highnes much wrong hinder reuenged knight let mee alone haue much hope ye strength arme giue good accompt therefore doo desire thée stand little side rosicleer woulde haue aunswered vpon sodaine saw comming parte pireo knight armed russet armour garnished stripe barres golde shield likewise russet painted god cupide two face valiant eleno prince dacia séeing controuersie betwixt three knight passed forward way saying vnto rosicleer without looking vpon armor deuice knight thou doost wrong disturbe first began battell rosicleer ye great anger wrath sée armor stranger power beholde deuice cousin blinde without anie consideration
